Ꞩirds zaur to to ihſtenu Tizzibu/ kas zaur to
Mihleſtibu ſpehziga irr/ ẜwehti man eekẜch tawas
Pateeẜibas/ taws Wahrds irr ta Pateeẜiba;
un pehz ẜcho Laiku eeẜchķiņko man to muhẜchigu
Dſihwoẜchanu/ ka es tur Tew pilnigi atſiht/ ſtattiht/
un pee Tew muhſchigi muhẜcham palikt warru/
zaur JESU Kriſtu/ tawu mihļu Dehlu/
muhẜu KUngu/ AMEN!
Gals/ Gohds DEewam!
